            <div class="column-center-inner">
             <div class="main section" id="main">
              <div class="widget Blog" id="Blog1">
               <div class="blog-posts hfeed">
                <!-- google_ad_section_start(name=default) -->
                <div class="date-outer">
                 <h2 class="date-header">
                  <span>
                   Tuesday, April 9, 2013
                  </span>
                 </h2>
                 <div class="date-posts">
                  <div class="post-outer">
                   <div class="post hentry">
                    <a name="2351971887938120381">
                    </a>
                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
                     Cinnamon Cream Cheese Roll-Ups
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-2351971887938120381">
                     <br/>
                     Holy lord. My mom emailed me this recipe last week, so I made it for the kids this weekend while The Dad was gone. Did I mention holy lord? Wow. They were
                     <i>
                      really
                     </i>
                     good hot out of the oven, but they didn't suck even a little bit the next day at room temp. I should rename them, White Girl Churros. 'Cause they're crispy. And taste fried. And have cinnamon and sugar smothered all over the outside of them. Sold yet? How's about some cream cheese frosting in the middle? Yeah, they're good. In fact, hang on a sec.....
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-yEdBSXoLyFw/UWL2u8JT2tI/AAAAAAAAV8U/A3J_XPPBkXY/s1600/Cinnamon+Cream+Cheese+Roll-Ups+036.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="266" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-yEdBSXoLyFw/UWL2u8JT2tI/AAAAAAAAV8U/A3J_XPPBkXY/s400/Cinnamon+Cream+Cheese+Roll-Ups+036.jpg" width="400"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <br/>
                     ...okay, I'm back. I decided I should be eating one while I write this post. As a service to you. And FYI, the one I'm chewing as my fingers type is straight outta the fridge and it
                     <i>
                      still
                     </i>
                     doesn't suck.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     Go here for the recipe:
                     <a href="http://fashionablyfoodie.com/2012/02/01/keshias-kakes-on-super-bowl-desserts/" target="_blank">
                      <span style="color: blue;">
                       <u>
                        <b>
                         Cinnamon Cream Cheese Roll-Ups
                        </b>
                       </u>
                      </span>
                     </a>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      Here they are coming together at my house:
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      Cream cheese and powdered sugar, aka, frosting.
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-42SncBUpoWc/UWL2mePqQXI/AAAAAAAAV6U/0WAhcI1BEaA/s1600/Cinnamon+Cream+Cheese+Roll-Ups+006.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="266" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-42SncBUpoWc/UWL2mePqQXI/AAAAAAAAV6U/0WAhcI1BEaA/s400/Cinnamon+Cream+Cheese+Roll-Ups+006.jpg" width="400"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <br/>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-JAYdAj1IZqE/UWL2nCI_CrI/AAAAAAAAV6k/-mgp3IryGLc/s1600/Cinnamon+Cream+Cheese+Roll-Ups+008.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="266" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-JAYdAj1IZqE/UWL2nCI_CrI/AAAAAAAAV6k/-mgp3IryGLc/s400/Cinnamon+Cream+Cheese+Roll-Ups+008.jpg" width="400"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <br/>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      Cinnamon and sugar.
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-boPbcgD_e3o/UWL2npHLyCI/AAAAAAAAV6s/o0QMo1khl38/s1600/Cinnamon+Cream+Cheese+Roll-Ups+010.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="317" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-boPbcgD_e3o/UWL2npHLyCI/AAAAAAAAV6s/o0QMo1khl38/s400/Cinnamon+Cream+Cheese+Roll-Ups+010.jpg" width="400"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <br/>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      White bread with the crust cut off and flattened with a rolling pin.
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      Yep, white bread.
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-kXWNQCIQDo4/UWL2oHYYpBI/AAAAAAAAV60/lq1WNG4O4ac/s1600/Cinnamon+Cream+Cheese+Roll-Ups+013.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="266" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-kXWNQCIQDo4/UWL2oHYYpBI/AAAAAAAAV60/lq1WNG4O4ac/s400/Cinnamon+Cream+Cheese+Roll-Ups+013.jpg" width="400"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <br/>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      Sweetened cream cheese spread on said bread.
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-Kif8nJqeFKo/UWL2pTyxKxI/AAAAAAAAV7E/Bit3bnCK36k/s1600/Cinnamon+Cream+Cheese+Roll-Ups+017.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="266" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-Kif8nJqeFKo/UWL2pTyxKxI/AAAAAAAAV7E/Bit3bnCK36k/s400/Cinnamon+Cream+Cheese+Roll-Ups+017.jpg" width="400"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      Rolled up and drowned in melted butter, then rolled in the cinnamon-sugar mix.
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-ZcO1NL2Cgp4/UWL2rLQt5bI/AAAAAAAAV7c/QyRqXmZplB8/s1600/Cinnamon+Cream+Cheese+Roll-Ups+024.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="400" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-ZcO1NL2Cgp4/UWL2rLQt5bI/AAAAAAAAV7c/QyRqXmZplB8/s400/Cinnamon+Cream+Cheese+Roll-Ups+024.jpg" width="266"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <br/>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-I8pBjAYHS8s/UWL2sSsFl3I/AAAAAAAAV7s/oZP5DmXgDLo/s1600/Cinnamon+Cream+Cheese+Roll-Ups+027.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="266" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-I8pBjAYHS8s/UWL2sSsFl3I/AAAAAAAAV7s/oZP5DmXgDLo/s400/Cinnamon+Cream+Cheese+Roll-Ups+027.jpg" width="400"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <br/>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-4S8EiKtz2LE/UWL2p4thGMI/AAAAAAAAV7M/vCtwSF521No/s1600/Cinnamon+Cream+Cheese+Roll-Ups+021.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="266" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-4S8EiKtz2LE/UWL2p4thGMI/AAAAAAAAV7M/vCtwSF521No/s400/Cinnamon+Cream+Cheese+Roll-Ups+021.jpg" width="400"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <br/>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-qCUx4brCK2o/UWL2tAzghEI/AAAAAAAAV70/uTEqPaEZD4c/s1600/Cinnamon+Cream+Cheese+Roll-Ups+028.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="266" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-qCUx4brCK2o/UWL2tAzghEI/AAAAAAAAV70/uTEqPaEZD4c/s400/Cinnamon+Cream+Cheese+Roll-Ups+028.jpg" width="400"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <br/>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      Baked until they're crispy and browned.
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      See all that crystallized butter and sugar around the outsides of all of them?
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      Yeah, you're gonna wanna eat that.
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-kS3eRr1RqtE/UWL2tojztwI/AAAAAAAAV78/NKpTiO_vngU/s1600/Cinnamon+Cream+Cheese+Roll-Ups+031.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="266" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-kS3eRr1RqtE/UWL2tojztwI/AAAAAAAAV78/NKpTiO_vngU/s400/Cinnamon+Cream+Cheese+Roll-Ups+031.jpg" width="400"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <br/>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-97XIR46fLxE/UWL2uGWd8_I/AAAAAAAAV8E/I8uBi2xrEkU/s1600/Cinnamon+Cream+Cheese+Roll-Ups+032.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="266" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-97XIR46fLxE/UWL2uGWd8_I/AAAAAAAAV8E/I8uBi2xrEkU/s400/Cinnamon+Cream+Cheese+Roll-Ups+032.jpg" width="400"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <br/>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/--o0cUnxc5qQ/UWL2ukyIs0I/AAAAAAAAV8M/PLlnklDeu5I/s1600/Cinnamon+Cream+Cheese+Roll-Ups+033.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="266" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/--o0cUnxc5qQ/UWL2ukyIs0I/AAAAAAAAV8M/PLlnklDeu5I/s400/Cinnamon+Cream+Cheese+Roll-Ups+033.jpg" width="400"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      Here's breakfast:
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-ORm13IQRZ7Y/UWL2w3iTV7I/AAAAAAAAV80/8ufF5xeSXig/s1600/Cinnamon+Cream+Cheese+Roll-Ups+040.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="400" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-ORm13IQRZ7Y/UWL2w3iTV7I/AAAAAAAAV80/8ufF5xeSXig/s400/Cinnamon+Cream+Cheese+Roll-Ups+040.jpg" width="266"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <br/>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      Did anyone notice the little face in the last picture?
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-10CAaIMETzY/UWL21cHM_ZI/AAAAAAAAV9U/zGMS3Vi3mxU/s1600/Cinnamon+Cream+Cheese+Roll-Ups+051.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="400" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-10CAaIMETzY/UWL21cHM_ZI/AAAAAAAAV9U/zGMS3Vi3mxU/s400/Cinnamon+Cream+Cheese+Roll-Ups+051.jpg" width="266"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <br/>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-yEdBSXoLyFw/UWL2u8JT2tI/AAAAAAAAV8U/A3J_XPPBkXY/s1600/Cinnamon+Cream+Cheese+Roll-Ups+036.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="266" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-yEdBSXoLyFw/UWL2u8JT2tI/AAAAAAAAV8U/A3J_XPPBkXY/s400/Cinnamon+Cream+Cheese+Roll-Ups+036.jpg" width="400"/>
                      </a>

                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">

                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-x_MM9_StUfc/UWL20e2aIFI/AAAAAAAAV9E/QT8QbIVWT30/s1600/Cinnamon+Cream+Cheese+Roll-Ups+042.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="266" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-x_MM9_StUfc/UWL20e2aIFI/AAAAAAAAV9E/QT8QbIVWT30/s400/Cinnamon+Cream+Cheese+Roll-Ups+042.jpg" width="400"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <br/>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-RAz7kwWAXsc/UWL22ZQLDJI/AAAAAAAAV9c/8IBkVxeUsXk/s1600/Cinnamon+Cream+Cheese+Roll-Ups+043.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="266" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-RAz7kwWAXsc/UWL22ZQLDJI/AAAAAAAAV9c/8IBkVxeUsXk/s400/Cinnamon+Cream+Cheese+Roll-Ups+043.jpg" width="400"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <br/>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-cXaQ9kjnWbs/UWL21AtxXlI/AAAAAAAAV9M/qWI2kdY22rI/s1600/Cinnamon+Cream+Cheese+Roll-Ups+045.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="266" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-cXaQ9kjnWbs/UWL21AtxXlI/AAAAAAAAV9M/qWI2kdY22rI/s400/Cinnamon+Cream+Cheese+Roll-Ups+045.jpg" width="400"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      These got more votes than the day before,
                      <a href="http://rindymae.blogspot.com/2013/04/apple-german-pancake-latest-meal-plan.html" target="_blank">
                       <span style="color: blue;">
                        <b>
                         Apple German Pancake
                        </b>
                       </span>
                      </a>
                      , breakfast from the little people, but really, who can blame them?
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      Before I go, as an FYI, the recipe calls for a 16oz loaf of bread.
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      Mine was 20-something ounces and I needed it all for the amount of cream cheese, and I still have some left over.
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      So either cut the cream cheese amount in half or plan on using more bread.
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      I also had cinnamon-sugar left over, but we use it for toast, so that didn't bother me.
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      You could cut it in half if you don't think you'll use the leftovers.
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      I'm off to eat another one.....
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>

                        <span style="font-size: x-small;">

                          parties I link up to.

                      </i>

                                 <div class="avatar-image-container">

                                 <div class="comment-block" id="c899310537590692553">
                                  <div class="comment-header" id="bc_0_21M" kind="m">
                                   <cite class="user blog-author">
                                    <a href="http://www.blogger.com/profile/07247379600555185331" rel="nofollow">
                                     Mindy
                                    </a>

                                   <span class="icon user blog-author">
                                   </span>
                                   <span class="datetime secondary-text">
                                    <a href="http://rindymae.blogspot.com/2013/04/cinnamon-cream-cheese-roll-ups.html?showComment=1367679662350#c899310537590692553" rel="nofollow">
                                     May 4, 2013 at 8:01 AM
                                    </a>
                                   </span>
                                  </div>
                                  <p class="comment-content" id="bc_0_21MC">
                                   A few of mine opened a bit toward the ends, and I think it was because the bread wasn't rolled out as big.  I've made them twice now and I think the key is to use really fresh bread and to make sure it's rolled out as large as you can get it.  The more times it's rolled over on itself, the less chance it has of opening.  Hope that helps!
                                  </p>

                            <p class="comment-content" id="bc_0_82MC">
                             I needed to make these ahead so I followed the directions until it came to dipping them in melted butter.  Instead I spread the regular butter onto the rolls, dipped them in the cinnamon mix, and placed them in a plastic container. I sprinkled a little extra cinnamon mix on each layer in the plastic container.  They turned out great...Phyllis.
                            </p>

                            </div>
                            <p class="comment-content" id="bc_0_100MC">
                             For those of you having trouble accessing the original recipe site, here ya go:
                             <br/>
                             <br/>
                             Ingredients
                             <br/>
                             1 loaf (16 ounces) thinly sliced white bread, crusts removed
                             <br/>
                             1 package (8 ounces) cream cheese, softened
                             <br/>
                             3/4 cup confectioners sugar
                             <br/>
                             1 cup sugar
                             <br/>
                             1-1/2 teaspoon ground cinnamon
                             <br/>
                             3/4 cup butter, melted
                             <br/>
                             <br/>
                             Directions
                             <br/>
                             <br/>
                             Flatten bread with a rolling-pin. In a bowl, combine cream cheese and confectioners sugar. In another bowl, combine sugar and cinnamon; set aside. Spread about 1 tablespoon of cheese mixture on each slice of bread. Roll up, jelly roll style. Dip in melted butter, then in cinnamon-sugar. Place on an ungreased baking sheet. Bake at 350 for 20 minutes or until golden brown. Yield: 16 roll-ups.
                            </p>
                            <span class="comment-actions secondary-text" id="bc_0_100MN" kind="m">
                             <a href="javascript:;" kind="i" o="r" target="_self">

               <div class="widget Profile" id="Profile1">
                <h2>
                 My Story
                </h2>
                <div class="widget-content">
                 <a href="http://www.blogger.com/profile/07247379600555185331">
                  <img alt="My Photo" class="profile-img" height="79" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Ji8_QGS14uA/UN58LeFLXmI/AAAAAAAARpI/Oj2GfJb17bs/s80/Profile%2BPic.jpg" width="80"/>
                 </a>
                 <dl class="profile-datablock">
                  <dt class="profile-data">
                   <a class="profile-name-link g-profile" href="http://www.blogger.com/profile/07247379600555185331" rel="author" style="background-image: url(//www.blogger.com/img/logo-16.png);">
                    Mindy
                   </a>
                  </dt>
                 </dl>
                 <a class="profile-link" href="http://www.blogger.com/profile/07247379600555185331" rel="author">
                  View my complete profile
                 </a>
                 <div class="clear">
                 </div>
                 <span class="widget-item-control">
                  <span class="item-control blog-admin">
                   <a class="quickedit" href="//www.blogger.com/rearrange?blogID=2733342915429018771&amp;widgetType=Profile&amp;widgetId=Profile1&amp;action=editWidget&amp;sectionId=sidebar-left-1" onclick='return _WidgetManager._PopupConfig(document.getElementById("Profile1"));' target="configProfile1" title="Edit">
                    <img alt="" height="18" src="//img1.blogblog.com/img/icon18_wrench_allbkg.png" width="18"/>
                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                 <div class="clear">
                 </div>
                </div>
               </div>
               <div class="widget Text" id="Text1">
                <div class="widget-content">
                 At the  most recent head count, my house consisted of The Mom (that would  be  me), The Dad, The Kid, The Girl, Baby, The Dog (in spirit), The Cat and The Tortoise.   I am completely obsessed with gardening, cooking and cheese.  If I was a superhero, my  name would be The Rearranger.   Saving the world, one knick knack at a  time. I'm a 39-year-old SAHM with a stockpile of photos and a head full of  ideas, ahem, ramblings.  Welcome to my life.
                </div>

                </div>
